## Race-by-Race ELO Changes

### Round 1 - Swiss Grand Prix
*Date: 1952-05-18*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 7 - Dutch Grand Prix
*Date: 1952-08-17*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting Elo | Change | New Elo | vs Teammate |
